	any_realm_province = {
	limit = { any_neighbor_province = { province = 1236 } }
	culture = romanoindian
	religion = vieti_orthodox
	remove_province_modifier = sold_off_land
            remove_province_modifier = thieves_guild
            remove_province_modifier = incompetent_rule
            remove_province_modifier = smugglers_ring
            remove_province_modifier = highway_robber_band
            remove_province_modifier = excessive_bureaucracy
            remove_province_modifier = peasant_unrest
            any_province_holding = {
                remove_holding_modifier = new_administration
                remove_holding_modifier = recently_conquered
                refill_holding_levy = yes
            }
	}
	any_realm_province = {
	limit = { any_neighbor_province = { province = 1318 } }
	culture = romanoindian
	religion = vieti_orthodox
	remove_province_modifier = sold_off_land
            remove_province_modifier = thieves_guild
            remove_province_modifier = incompetent_rule
            remove_province_modifier = smugglers_ring
            remove_province_modifier = highway_robber_band
            remove_province_modifier = excessive_bureaucracy
            remove_province_modifier = peasant_unrest
            any_province_holding = {
                remove_holding_modifier = new_administration
                remove_holding_modifier = recently_conquered
                refill_holding_levy = yes
            }
	}
	}
}


# Hereclemasculist Caste System
character_event = {
	id = indoromans.2222
	hide_window = yes	
	min_age = 14
	
	trigger = {
	    religion = hereclemasculist_pagan
		age = 14
		NOR = { 
		has_character_modifier = debug_elder_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_first_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_second_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_third_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_fourth_hmasc_caste
		
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	
	if = {
	limit = {
	is_female = no
	age = 50
	NOR = {
	AND = {
	trait = homosexual
	NOT = { 
	OR = {
	trait = strong 
	combat_rating = 50
	}
	}
	}
	trait = craven
	trait = weak
	trait = feeble
	trait = eunuch
	}
	}
	add_character_modifier = { 
	name = debug_elder_hmasc_caste
	duration = -1
	}
	}
	
	if = {
	limit = {
	is_female = yes
	OR = {
	has_education_martial_trigger = yes
	combat_rating = 50
	}
	OR = {
	trait = robust
	trait = independent
	trait = chad_thundercock #patrician trait from the personal mod
	trait = crusader
	trait = mujahid
	trait = eagle_warrior
	trait = sun_warrior
	trait = ukkos_shield
	trait = nyames_shield
	trait = peruns_chosen
	trait = romuvas_own
	trait = ares_own
	trait = tengri_warrior
	trait = shaddai
	trait = gondi_shahansha
	trait = kailash_guardian
	trait = valhalla_bound
	trait = ravager
	trait = sea_queen
	trait = shieldmaiden
	trait = strong
	trait = duelist
	trait = falconer
	trait = trained_warrior
	trait = skilled_warrior
	trait = master_warrior
	}
	}
	add_character_modifier = { 
	name = debug_first_hmasc_caste
	duration = -1
	}
	}
	
	if = {
	limit = {
	NOT = { age = 50 }
	is_female = no
	NOR = {
	AND = {
	trait = homosexual
	NOT = { 
	OR = {
	trait = strong 
	combat_rating = 50
	}
	}
	}
	trait = craven
	trait = weak
	trait = feeble
	trait = eunuch
	}
	}
	add_character_modifier = { 
	name = debug_first_hmasc_caste
	duration = -1
	}
	}
	
	if = {
	limit = {
	is_female = yes
	NOT = {
	OR = {
	has_education_martial_trigger = yes
	combat_rating = 50
	}
	OR = {
	trait = robust
	trait = independent
	trait = chad_thundercock #patrician trait from the personal mod
	trait = crusader
	trait = mujahid
	trait = eagle_warrior
	trait = sun_warrior
	trait = ukkos_shield
	trait = nyames_shield
	trait = peruns_chosen
	trait = romuvas_own
	trait = ares_own
	trait = tengri_warrior
	trait = shaddai
	trait = gondi_shahansha
	trait = kailash_guardian
	trait = valhalla_bound
	trait = ravager
	trait = sea_queen
	trait = shieldmaiden
	trait = strong
	trait = duelist
	trait = falconer
	trait = trained_warrior
	trait = skilled_warrior
	trait = master_warrior
	}
	}
	}
	add_character_modifier = { 
	name = debug_second_hmasc_caste
	duration = -1
	}
	}
	
	if = {
	limit = {
	is_female = no
	NOT = {
	trait = eunuch
	}
	OR = {
	AND = {
	trait = homosexual
	NOT = { 
	OR = {
	trait = strong 
	combat_rating = 50
	}
	}

	trait = weak
	trait = feeble

	min_age = 14

	    NOT = { religion = hereclemasculist_pagan }
		OR = { 
		has_character_modifier = debug_elder_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_first_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_second_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_third_hmasc_caste
		has_character_modifier = debug_fourth_hmasc_caste
		
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	remove_character_modifier = debug_elder_hmasc_caste
	remove_character_modifier = debug_first_hmasc_caste
	remove_character_modifier = debug_second_hmasc_caste
	remove_character_modifier = debug_third_hmasc_caste
	remove_character_modifier = debug_fourth_hmasc_caste
	
	}
}
